     1	#' Integrate TRISK PD shift into an internal PD estimate
     2	#'
     3	#' Applies one of three methods to translate the TRISK baseline-to-shock PD
     4	#' change into the bank's own internal PD scale. Mirrors the logic in the
     5	#' trisk.r.docker Shiny integration module.
     6	#'
     7	#' @param analysis_data Data frame from [run_trisk_on_portfolio()]; must contain
     8	#'   columns `pd_baseline`, `pd_shock`.
     9	#' @param internal_pd Either (a) a numeric vector of length `nrow(analysis_data)`,
    10	#'   (b) a data frame with `company_id` and `internal_pd` columns, or (c) NULL
    11	#'   (default) in which case `pd_baseline` is used.
    12	#' @param method One of "zscore", "absolute", "relative". Default "zscore"
    13	#'   (Merton-style probit recombination of default thresholds, not the Basel
    14	#'   IRB/Vasicek formula; zero-safe via clipping; recommended for sparse
    15	#'   portfolios where baseline PDs can underflow from Merton inputs).
    16	#' @param zscore_floor Lower clip bound for PDs before `qnorm()` in the zscore
    17	#'   method. Default 1e-4.
    18	#' @param zscore_cap Upper clip bound. Default 1 - 1e-4.
    19	#'
    20	#' @return A list with three elements:
    21	#' \describe{
    22	#'   \item{portfolio}{`analysis_data` with columns added: `internal_pd`,
    23	#'     `pd_change`, `pd_change_pct`, `trisk_adjusted_pd`, `pd_adjustment`.}
    24	#'   \item{portfolio_long}{Pivot-longer helper for plotting.}
    25	#'   \item{aggregate}{One-row tibble of EAD-weighted portfolio metrics.}
    26	#' }
    27	#' @export
    28	integrate_pd <- function(analysis_data,
    29	                         internal_pd = NULL,
    30	                         method = c("zscore", "absolute", "relative"),
    31	                         zscore_floor = ZSCORE_FLOOR_DEFAULT,
    32	                         zscore_cap = ZSCORE_CAP_DEFAULT) {
    33	  method <- match.arg(method)
    34	
    35	  if (nrow(analysis_data) == 0) {
    36	    stop("integrate_pd(): analysis_data has zero rows; nothing to integrate.")
    37	  }
    38	
    39	  if (zscore_floor >= zscore_cap) {
    40	    stop("integrate_pd(): zscore_floor must be strictly less than zscore_cap (got ",
    41	         zscore_floor, " vs ", zscore_cap, ")")
    42	  }
    43	
    44	  required_cols <- c("pd_baseline", "pd_shock")
    45	  missing_cols <- setdiff(required_cols, colnames(analysis_data))
    46	  if (length(missing_cols) > 0) {
    47	    stop("integrate_pd(): missing required columns in analysis_data: ",
    48	         paste(missing_cols, collapse = ", "))
    49	  }
    50	
    51	  internal_vec <- resolve_internal_series(analysis_data, internal_pd, "pd_baseline")
    52	  if (all(is.na(internal_vec))) {
    53	    stop("integrate_pd(): all resolved internal PD values are NA.")
    54	  }
    55	
    56	  pd_baseline <- analysis_data$pd_baseline
    57	  pd_shock <- analysis_data$pd_shock
    58	  pd_change <- pd_shock - pd_baseline
    59	  pd_change_pct <- ifelse(pd_baseline != 0, pd_change / pd_baseline, NA_real_)
    60	
    61	  # R1: the relative method no-ops on zero-baseline rows (change_pct forced to 0),
    62	  # silently dropping the shock signal. Surface it.
    63	  if (method == "relative") {
    64	    n_zero <- sum(pd_baseline == 0, na.rm = TRUE)
    65	    if (n_zero > 0) {
    66	      warning("integrate_pd(): method 'relative' leaves ", n_zero,
    67	              " row(s) with pd_baseline == 0 unchanged (shock signal dropped); ",
    68	              "use 'absolute' or 'zscore' for those.", call. = FALSE)
    69	    }
    70	  }
    71	
    72	  adjusted <- apply_pd_method(internal_vec, pd_baseline, pd_shock,
    73	                              method, zscore_floor, zscore_cap)
    74	  adjusted <- pmin(pmax(adjusted, 0), 1)
    75	
    76	  portfolio <- analysis_data |>
    77	    dplyr::mutate(
    78	      internal_pd        = internal_vec,
    79	      pd_change          = pd_change,
    80	      pd_change_pct      = pd_change_pct,
    81	      trisk_adjusted_pd  = adjusted,
    82	      pd_adjustment      = adjusted - internal_vec
    83	    )
    84	
    85	  portfolio_long <- portfolio |>
    86	    tidyr::pivot_longer(
    87	      cols = dplyr::all_of(c("internal_pd", "pd_baseline", "pd_shock", "trisk_adjusted_pd")),
    88	      names_to = "pd_type_raw",
    89	      values_to = "pd_value"
    90	    ) |>
    91	    dplyr::mutate(
    92	      pd_type = ordered(
    93	        dplyr::case_when(
    94	          .data$pd_type_raw == "internal_pd"       ~ "internal",
    95	          .data$pd_type_raw == "pd_baseline"       ~ "baseline",
    96	          .data$pd_type_raw == "pd_shock"          ~ "shock",
    97	          .data$pd_type_raw == "trisk_adjusted_pd" ~ "trisk_adjusted"
    98	        ),
    99	        levels = c("internal", "baseline", "shock", "trisk_adjusted")
   100	      )
   101	    ) |>
   102	    dplyr::select(-"pd_type_raw")
   103	
   104	  aggregate <- aggregate_pd_integration(portfolio)
   105	  if (method == "zscore") {
   106	    clipped <- zscore_clipped_share(list(internal_vec, pd_baseline, pd_shock),
   107	                                    zscore_floor, zscore_cap)
   108	    aggregate$zscore_clipped_share <- clipped
   109	    warn_if_overclipped(clipped, "integrate_pd")
   110	  }
   111	
   112	  list(
   113	    portfolio = portfolio,
   114	    portfolio_long = portfolio_long,
   115	    aggregate = aggregate
   116	  )
   117	}
   118	
   119	#' Aggregate PD integration results to EAD-weighted portfolio level
   120	#'
   121	#' @param portfolio_df The `$portfolio` element from [integrate_pd()], containing
   122	#'   `internal_pd`, `pd_baseline`, `pd_shock`, `trisk_adjusted_pd`,
   123	#'   `exposure_value_usd`.
   124	#' @param group_cols Character vector of columns to group by. NULL (default) produces
   125	#'   a single-row portfolio total. Pass e.g. "sector" for a sector rollup.
   126	#'
   127	#' @return A one-row tibble (per group) with EAD-weighted PD metrics.
   128	#' @export
   129	aggregate_pd_integration <- function(portfolio_df, group_cols = NULL) {
   130	  required <- c("internal_pd", "pd_baseline", "pd_shock",
   131	                "trisk_adjusted_pd", "exposure_value_usd")
   132	  missing_cols <- setdiff(required, colnames(portfolio_df))
   133	  if (length(missing_cols) > 0) {
   134	    stop("aggregate_pd_integration(): missing required columns: ",
   135	         paste(missing_cols, collapse = ", "))
   136	  }
   137	
   138	  grouped <- if (is.null(group_cols)) {
   139	    portfolio_df |> dplyr::mutate(.dummy = 1L) |> dplyr::group_by(.data$.dummy)
   140	  } else {
   141	    portfolio_df |> dplyr::group_by(dplyr::across(dplyr::all_of(group_cols)))
   142	  }
   143	
   144	  agg <- grouped |>
   145	    dplyr::summarise(
   146	      total_exposure_usd   = sum(.data$exposure_value_usd, na.rm = TRUE),
   147	      weighted_pd_internal = sum(.data$internal_pd       * .data$exposure_value_usd, na.rm = TRUE),
   148	      weighted_pd_baseline = sum(.data$pd_baseline       * .data$exposure_value_usd, na.rm = TRUE),
   149	      weighted_pd_shock    = sum(.data$pd_shock          * .data$exposure_value_usd, na.rm = TRUE),
   150	      weighted_pd_adjusted = sum(.data$trisk_adjusted_pd * .data$exposure_value_usd, na.rm = TRUE),
   151	      .groups = "drop"
   152	    ) |>
   153	    dplyr::mutate(
   154	      weighted_pd_internal   = .data$weighted_pd_internal / .data$total_exposure_usd,
   155	      weighted_pd_baseline   = .data$weighted_pd_baseline / .data$total_exposure_usd,
   156	      weighted_pd_shock      = .data$weighted_pd_shock    / .data$total_exposure_usd,
   157	      weighted_pd_adjusted   = .data$weighted_pd_adjusted / .data$total_exposure_usd,
   158	      weighted_pd_adjustment     = .data$weighted_pd_adjusted - .data$weighted_pd_internal,
   159	      weighted_pd_adjustment_pct = dplyr::if_else(
   160	        !is.na(.data$weighted_pd_internal) & .data$weighted_pd_internal != 0,
   161	        .data$weighted_pd_adjustment / .data$weighted_pd_internal,
   162	        NA_real_
   163	      )
   164	    )
   165	
   166	  if (is.null(group_cols)) {
   167	    agg <- agg |> dplyr::select(-dplyr::any_of(".dummy"))
   168	  }
   169	
   170	  tibble::as_tibble(agg)
   171	}
   172	
   173	# Internal - resolve the internal PD/EL series from vector, df, or NULL input.
   174	resolve_internal_series <- function(analysis_data, user_values, default_col) {
   175	  n <- nrow(analysis_data)
   176	  default_vec <- analysis_data[[default_col]]
   177	
   178	  if (is.null(user_values)) {
   179	    return(default_vec)
   180	  }
   181	
   182	  if (is.numeric(user_values)) {
   183	    if (length(user_values) != n) {
   184	      stop("resolve_internal_series(): vector length ", length(user_values),
   185	           " does not match nrow(analysis_data) = ", n)
   186	    }
   187	    return(user_values)
   188	  }
   189	
   190	  if (is.data.frame(user_values)) {
   191	    if (!"company_id" %in% colnames(user_values)) {
   192	      stop("resolve_internal_series(): dataframe must have 'company_id' and one value column.",
   193	           call. = FALSE)
   194	    }
   195	    # Identify join keys by a known identifier set (NOT by "absent from
   196	    # analysis_data" — the value column name, e.g. internal_pd, can ride along in
   197	    # analysis_data from the portfolio input). The value column is whatever
   198	    # remains. Matching on ALL shared keys (CX1) prevents a per-(company, term)
   199	    # lookup from collapsing onto the first company_id match.
   200	    id_candidates <- c("company_id", "term", "sector", "technology",
   201	                       "country_iso2", "run_id")
   202	    key_cols <- intersect(colnames(user_values), id_candidates)
   203	    val_cols <- setdiff(colnames(user_values), key_cols)
   204	    if (length(val_cols) != 1) {
   205	      stop("resolve_internal_series(): user_values must have exactly one value ",
   206	           "(non-key) column; found: ", paste(val_cols, collapse = ", "), ".",
   207	           call. = FALSE)
   208	    }
   209	    val_col <- val_cols[1]
   210	    # Join only on keys that actually exist in analysis_data.
   211	    key_cols <- intersect(key_cols, colnames(analysis_data))
   212	    # Ambiguity guard: duplicate keys would apply the first match to every
   213	    # analysis row sharing that key. Force the caller to disambiguate.
   214	    if (anyDuplicated(user_values[key_cols]) > 0L) {
   215	      stop("resolve_internal_series(): user_values has duplicate rows for key(s) (",
   216	           paste(key_cols, collapse = ", "),
   217	           "); include a disambiguating column (e.g. 'term') so each row maps to a ",
   218	           "unique value, or supply one row per company_id.", call. = FALSE)
   219	    }
   220	    # Composite key match across all key columns (character-coerced for type-safe
   221	    # joins; \r separator avoids collisions between concatenated key parts).
   222	    make_key <- function(df) {
   223	      do.call(paste, c(lapply(key_cols, function(k) as.character(df[[k]])), sep = "\r"))
   224	    }
   225	    out <- default_vec
   226	    idx <- match(make_key(analysis_data), make_key(user_values))
   227	    unmatched_ids <- unique(as.character(analysis_data$company_id)[is.na(idx)])
   228	    if (length(unmatched_ids) > 0) {
   229	      warning(
   230	        "resolve_internal_series(): ", length(unmatched_ids),
   231	        " company_id(s) in analysis_data not matched in user_values; ",
   232	        "falling back to '", default_col, "' for those rows. Unmatched: ",
   233	        paste(unmatched_ids, collapse = ", "),
   234	        call. = FALSE
   235	      )
   236	    }
   237	    out[!is.na(idx)] <- user_values[[val_col]][idx[!is.na(idx)]]
   238	    return(out)
   239	  }
   240	
   241	  stop("resolve_internal_series(): user_values must be NULL, numeric vector, or data frame.")
   242	}
   243	
   244	# Internal (Z1) - fraction of rows where any input PD lies outside [floor, cap]
   245	# and is therefore clamped before qnorm(). A high share means the z-score overlay
   246	# reflects the clip bound, not the model. Rows that are all-NA across the series
   247	# are excluded from the denominator (they carry no model signal to clip).
   248	zscore_clipped_share <- function(series_list, floor, cap) {
   249	  if (length(series_list) == 0 || length(series_list[[1]]) == 0) return(NA_real_)
   250	  all_na  <- Reduce(`&`, lapply(series_list, is.na))
   251	  clipped <- Reduce(`|`, lapply(series_list, function(x) {
   252	    !is.na(x) & (x < floor | x > cap)
   253	  }))
   254	  valid <- !all_na
   255	  if (!any(valid)) return(NA_real_)
   256	  mean(clipped[valid])
   257	}
   258	
   259	# Internal (Z1) - warn when the clipped share crosses the threshold.
   260	warn_if_overclipped <- function(share, fn) {
   261	  if (!is.na(share) && share > ZSCORE_CLIP_WARN_THRESHOLD) {
   262	    warning(
   263	      fn, "(): ", round(share * 100), "% of rows have a PD clipped to the ",
   264	      "z-score floor/cap before qnorm(); the overlay is governed by the clip ",
   265	      "bound, not the model. Baseline PDs below the floor erase the shock signal. ",
   266	      "Consider method = \"absolute\" for underflow-prone (e.g. IG / short-horizon) ",
   267	      "books, or review zscore_floor.",
   268	      call. = FALSE
   269	    )
   270	  }
   271	  invisible(share)
   272	}
   273	
   274	# Internal - pure vector math for the three PD methods. Shiny-parity.
   275	apply_pd_method <- function(internal, baseline, shock, method,
   276	                            zscore_floor, zscore_cap) {
   277	  switch(method,
   278	    absolute = internal + (shock - baseline),
   279	    relative = {
   280	      change_pct <- ifelse(baseline != 0, (shock - baseline) / baseline, 0)
   281	      internal * (1 + change_pct)
   282	    },
   283	    zscore = {
   284	      clip <- function(x) pmin(pmax(x, zscore_floor), zscore_cap)
   285	      z_internal <- stats::qnorm(clip(internal))
   286	      z_baseline <- stats::qnorm(clip(baseline))
   287	      z_shock    <- stats::qnorm(clip(shock))
   288	      stats::pnorm(z_internal + z_shock - z_baseline)
   289	    }
   290	  )
   291	}
   292	
   293	#' Integrate TRISK EL shift into an internal EL estimate
   294	#'
   295	#' Applies one of three methods to translate the TRISK baseline-to-shock EL
   296	#' change into the bank's own internal EL scale. "absolute" and "relative"
   297	#' mirror the Shiny EL integration logic; "zscore" adds a Basel IRB-aligned
   298	#' Vasicek recombination by transforming EL to an effective PD
   299	#' (|EL| / (EAD * LGD)), applying the z-score combination in normal-quantile
   300	#' space, and converting back. All three methods return EL as a positive
   301	#' magnitude (post 59571f3 package-wide convention). The zscore method requires
   302	#' `exposure_value_usd` and `loss_given_default` columns in `analysis_data`.
   303	#'
   304	#' @param analysis_data Data frame from [run_trisk_on_portfolio()]; must contain
   305	#'   columns `expected_loss_baseline`, `expected_loss_shock`. The zscore method
   306	#'   additionally needs an EAD denominator: it uses an `exposure_at_default`
   307	#'   column when present (the canonical contract, written by
   308	#'   [compute_analysis_metrics()] and [run_trisk_on_simple_portfolio()]) and
   309	#'   otherwise reconstructs it as `exposure_value_usd * loss_given_default`.
   310	#' @param internal_el Numeric vector of length `nrow(analysis_data)`, or a data
   311	#'   frame with `company_id` + `internal_el` columns, or NULL (default) which
   312	#'   uses `expected_loss_baseline`.
   313	#' @param method One of "zscore", "absolute", "relative". Default "zscore".
   314	#' @param zscore_floor Lower clip bound for effective PDs before `qnorm()`.
   315	#'   Default 1e-4.
   316	#' @param zscore_cap Upper clip bound. Default 1 - 1e-4.
   317	#'
   318	#' @return List with `$portfolio`, `$portfolio_long`, `$aggregate`.
   319	#' @export
   320	integrate_el <- function(analysis_data,
   321	                         internal_el = NULL,
   322	                         method = c("zscore", "absolute", "relative"),
   323	                         zscore_floor = ZSCORE_FLOOR_DEFAULT,
   324	                         zscore_cap = ZSCORE_CAP_DEFAULT) {
   325	  method <- match.arg(method)
   326	
   327	  if (nrow(analysis_data) == 0) {
   328	    stop("integrate_el(): analysis_data has zero rows; nothing to integrate.")
   329	  }
   330	
   331	  if (zscore_floor >= zscore_cap) {
   332	    stop("integrate_el(): zscore_floor must be strictly less than zscore_cap (got ",
   333	         zscore_floor, " vs ", zscore_cap, ")")
   334	  }
   335	
   336	  required_cols <- c("expected_loss_baseline", "expected_loss_shock")
   337	  missing_cols <- setdiff(required_cols, colnames(analysis_data))
   338	  if (length(missing_cols) > 0) {
   339	    stop("integrate_el(): missing required columns: ",
   340	         paste(missing_cols, collapse = ", "))
   341	  }
   342	  if (method == "zscore") {
   343	    # Need EAD: either an explicit exposure_at_default column, or the
   344	    # ingredients (exposure_value_usd + loss_given_default) to reconstruct it.
   345	    has_ead     <- "exposure_at_default" %in% colnames(analysis_data)
   346	    has_product <- all(c("exposure_value_usd", "loss_given_default")
   347	                       %in% colnames(analysis_data))
   348	    if (!has_ead && !has_product) {
   349	      stop("integrate_el(): zscore method needs either `exposure_at_default` ",
   350	           "or both `exposure_value_usd` + `loss_given_default` in analysis_data.")
   351	    }
   352	  }
   353	
   354	  internal_vec <- resolve_internal_series(analysis_data, internal_el,
   355	                                          "expected_loss_baseline")
   356	  if (all(is.na(internal_vec))) {
   357	    stop("integrate_el(): all resolved internal EL values are NA.")
   358	  }
   359	
   360	  el_baseline <- analysis_data$expected_loss_baseline
   361	  el_shock <- analysis_data$expected_loss_shock
   362	  el_change <- el_shock - el_baseline
   363	  el_change_pct <- ifelse(el_baseline != 0, el_change / el_baseline, NA_real_)
   364	
   365	  # R1: the relative method no-ops on zero-baseline rows. Surface it.
   366	  if (method == "relative") {
   367	    n_zero <- sum(el_baseline == 0, na.rm = TRUE)
   368	    if (n_zero > 0) {
   369	      warning("integrate_el(): method 'relative' leaves ", n_zero,
   370	              " row(s) with expected_loss_baseline == 0 unchanged (shock signal ",
   371	              "dropped); use 'absolute' or 'zscore' for those.", call. = FALSE)
   372	    }
   373	  }
   374	
   375	  # zscore needs an EAD denominator. Prefer an explicit exposure_at_default
   376	  # column when the caller has supplied one (e.g. via compute_analysis_metrics
   377	  # or run_trisk_on_simple_portfolio, which scale EAD by NPV share). Falling
   378	  # back to exposure_value_usd * loss_given_default is correct only when the
   379	  # EL columns are on that same unscaled basis; otherwise the effective-PD
   380	  # round-trip recovers a scaled PD and the z-score result is wrong.
   381	  ead <- if (method == "zscore") {
   382	    if ("exposure_at_default" %in% colnames(analysis_data)) {
   383	      analysis_data$exposure_at_default
   384	    } else {
   385	      analysis_data$exposure_value_usd * analysis_data$loss_given_default
   386	    }
   387	  } else NULL
   388	
   389	  adjusted <- apply_el_method(internal_vec, el_baseline, el_shock, method,
   390	                              ead          = ead,
   391	                              zscore_floor = zscore_floor,
   392	                              zscore_cap   = zscore_cap)
   393	
   394	  portfolio <- analysis_data |>
   395	    dplyr::mutate(
   396	      internal_el        = internal_vec,
   397	      el_change          = el_change,
   398	      el_change_pct      = el_change_pct,
   399	      trisk_adjusted_el  = adjusted,
   400	      el_adjustment      = adjusted - internal_vec
   401	    )
   402	
   403	  portfolio_long <- portfolio |>
   404	    tidyr::pivot_longer(
   405	      cols = dplyr::all_of(c("internal_el", "expected_loss_baseline",
   406	                             "expected_loss_shock", "trisk_adjusted_el")),
   407	      names_to = "el_type_raw",
   408	      values_to = "el_value"
   409	    ) |>
   410	    dplyr::mutate(
   411	      el_type = factor(
   412	        dplyr::case_when(
   413	          .data$el_type_raw == "internal_el"            ~ "internal",
   414	          .data$el_type_raw == "expected_loss_baseline" ~ "baseline",
   415	          .data$el_type_raw == "expected_loss_shock"    ~ "shock",
   416	          .data$el_type_raw == "trisk_adjusted_el"      ~ "trisk_adjusted"
   417	        ),
   418	        levels = c("internal", "baseline", "shock", "trisk_adjusted")
   419	      )
   420	    ) |>
   421	    dplyr::select(-"el_type_raw")
   422	
   423	  aggregate <- aggregate_el_integration(portfolio)
   424	  if (method == "zscore") {
   425	    # Effective PD = |EL| / EAD, matching apply_el_method(). Rows with EAD <= 0
   426	    # carry no loss and contribute 0 EL; map them to NA so they are excluded from
   427	    # the clip-share denominator rather than counting as clipped (warning misfire).
   428	    eff_pd <- function(x) ifelse(!is.na(ead) & ead > 0, abs(x) / ead, NA_real_)
   429	    clipped <- zscore_clipped_share(
   430	      list(eff_pd(internal_vec), eff_pd(el_baseline), eff_pd(el_shock)),
   431	      zscore_floor, zscore_cap
   432	    )
   433	    aggregate$zscore_clipped_share <- clipped
   434	    warn_if_overclipped(clipped, "integrate_el")
   435	  }
   436	
   437	  list(
   438	    portfolio = portfolio,
   439	    portfolio_long = portfolio_long,
   440	    aggregate = aggregate
   441	  )
   442	}
   443	
   444	apply_el_method <- function(internal, baseline, shock, method,
   445	                            ead = NULL,
   446	                            zscore_floor = ZSCORE_FLOOR_DEFAULT,
   447	                            zscore_cap = ZSCORE_CAP_DEFAULT) {
   448	  switch(method,
   449	    absolute = internal + (shock - baseline),
   450	    relative = {

exec

 #' @return A named list with:
 #' \itemize{
 #'   \item \code{portfolio_results_tech_detail}: company/term/sector/technology-level details.
 #'   \item \code{portfolio_results}: portfolio-level results re-aggregated to input-row shape.
 #' }
 #' @export

 run_trisk_on_simple_portfolio <- function(assets_data,
                                          scenarios_data,
                                          financial_data,
                                          carbon_data,
                                          portfolio_data,
                                          baseline_scenario,
                                          target_scenario,
                                          ...) {

     dplyr::mutate(
       asset_id = as.character(.data$asset_id),
       company_id = as.character(.data$company_id)
     )
   financial_data <- financial_data |>
     dplyr::mutate(company_id = as.character(.data$company_id))
 
   portfolio_data <- portfolio_data |>
     dplyr::mutate(

     )
 
   check_portfolio_simple(portfolio_data)
+  warn_scenario_family_mismatch(baseline_scenario, target_scenario)  # NM1

   portfolio_matched_companies <- portfolio_data |>
     dplyr::filter(!is.na(.data$company_id)) |>
     dplyr::distinct(.data$company_id) |>

     )

   cat("-- Start Trisk")
   st_results <- trisk.model::run_trisk_model(

     financial_data = financial_data,

   npv_results <- st_results$npv_results |>

 # Internal - resolve the internal PD/EL series from vector, df, or NULL input.
 resolve_internal_series <- function(analysis_data, user_values, default_col) {
   n <- nrow(analysis_data)
   default_vec <- analysis_data[[default_col]]
 
   if (is.null(user_values)) {
     return(default_vec)
   }
 
   if (is.numeric(user_values)) {
     if (length(user_values) != n) {
       stop("resolve_internal_series(): vector length ", length(user_values),
            " does not match nrow(analysis_data) = ", n)
     }

+      stop("resolve_internal_series(): dataframe must have 'company_id' and one value column.",
+           call. = FALSE)
+    }
+    # Identify join keys by a known identifier set (NOT by "absent from
+    # analysis_data" — the value column name, e.g. internal_pd, can ride along in
+    # analysis_data from the portfolio input). The value column is whatever
+    # remains. Matching on ALL shared keys (CX1) prevents a per-(company, term)
+    # lookup from collapsing onto the first company_id match.
+    id_candidates <- c("company_id", "term", "sector", "technology",
+                       "country_iso2", "run_id")
+    key_cols <- intersect(colnames(user_values), id_candidates)
+    val_cols <- setdiff(colnames(user_values), key_cols)
+    if (length(val_cols) != 1) {
+      stop("resolve_internal_series(): user_values must have exactly one value ",
+           "(non-key) column; found: ", paste(val_cols, collapse = ", "), ".",
+           call. = FALSE)
+    }
+    val_col <- val_cols[1]
+    # Join only on keys that actually exist in analysis_data.
+    key_cols <- intersect(key_cols, colnames(analysis_data))
+    # Ambiguity guard: duplicate keys would apply the first match to every
+    # analysis row sharing that key. Force the caller to disambiguate.
+    if (anyDuplicated(user_values[key_cols]) > 0L) {
+      stop("resolve_internal_series(): user_values has duplicate rows for key(s) (",
+           paste(key_cols, collapse = ", "),
+           "); include a disambiguating column (e.g. 'term') so each row maps to a ",
+           "unique value, or supply one row per company_id.", call. = FALSE)
+    }
+    # Composite key match across all key columns (character-coerced for type-safe
+    # joins; \r separator avoids collisions between concatenated key parts).
+    make_key <- function(df) {

         "resolve_internal_series(): ", length(unmatched_ids),

         "falling back to '", default_col, "' for those rows. Unmatched: ",
         paste(unmatched_ids, collapse = ", "),
         call. = FALSE
       )
     }
     out[!is.na(idx)] <- user_values[[val_col]][idx[!is.na(idx)]]
     return(out)
   }
 
   stop("resolve_internal_series(): user_values must be NULL, numeric vector, or data frame.")

+# Internal (Z1) - fraction of rows where any input PD lies outside [floor, cap]
+# and is therefore clamped before qnorm(). A high share means the z-score overlay
+# reflects the clip bound, not the model. Rows that are all-NA across the series
+# are excluded from the denominator (they carry no model signal to clip).
+zscore_clipped_share <- function(series_list, floor, cap) {
+  if (length(series_list) == 0 || length(series_list[[1]]) == 0) return(NA_real_)
+  all_na  <- Reduce(`&`, lapply(series_list, is.na))
+  clipped <- Reduce(`|`, lapply(series_list, function(x) {
+    !is.na(x) & (x < floor | x > cap)
+  }))
+  valid <- !all_na
+  if (!any(valid)) return(NA_real_)
+  mean(clipped[valid])
+}
+
+# Internal (Z1) - warn when the clipped share crosses the threshold.
+warn_if_overclipped <- function(share, fn) {
+  if (!is.na(share) && share > ZSCORE_CLIP_WARN_THRESHOLD) {
+    warning(
+      fn, "(): ", round(share * 100), "% of rows have a PD clipped to the ",
+      "z-score floor/cap before qnorm(); the overlay is governed by the clip ",
+      "bound, not the model. Baseline PDs below the floor erase the shock signal. ",
+      "Consider method = \"absolute\" for underflow-prone (e.g. IG / short-horizon) ",
+      "books, or review zscore_floor.",
+      call. = FALSE
+    )
+  }
+  invisible(share)
+}
+
 # Internal - pure vector math for the three PD methods. Shiny-parity.
 apply_pd_method <- function(internal, baseline, shock, method,
                             zscore_floor, zscore_cap) {
   switch(method,
     absolute = internal + (shock - baseline),
     relative = {
       change_pct <- ifelse(baseline != 0, (shock - baseline) / baseline, 0)
       internal * (1 + change_pct)
     },
     zscore = {
       clip <- function(x) pmin(pmax(x, zscore_floor), zscore_cap)
       z_internal <- stats::qnorm(clip(internal))
       z_baseline <- stats::qnorm(clip(baseline))
       z_shock    <- stats::qnorm(clip(shock))
       stats::pnorm(z_internal + z_shock - z_baseline)
     }
   )
 }
 
 #' Integrate TRISK EL shift into an internal EL estimate
 #'
 #' Applies one of three methods to translate the TRISK baseline-to-shock EL

 #' magnitude (post 59571f3 package-wide convention). The zscore method requires
 #' `exposure_value_usd` and `loss_given_default` columns in `analysis_data`.
 #'

 apply_el_method <- function(internal, baseline, shock, method,
                             ead = NULL,
                             zscore_floor = ZSCORE_FLOOR_DEFAULT,
                             zscore_cap = ZSCORE_CAP_DEFAULT) {
   switch(method,
     absolute = internal + (shock - baseline),
     relative = {
       change_pct <- ifelse(baseline != 0, (shock - baseline) / baseline, 0)
       internal * (1 + change_pct)
     },
     zscore = {
       # Basel IRB style recombination, applied to EL via the
       # effective-PD transform: EL = EAD * PD  -->  PD_eff = |EL| / EAD,
       # where `ead` is exposure_value_usd * loss_given_default. After z-score
       # recombination in normal-quantile space, convert back via EAD * PD_adj.
       # Returns a positive magnitude, matching the package's positive-EL
       # convention (see 59571f3).
       clip <- function(x) pmin(pmax(x, zscore_floor), zscore_cap)
       safe_div <- function(x) ifelse(ead > 0, abs(x) / ead, 0)
       pd_internal <- clip(safe_div(internal))
       pd_baseline <- clip(safe_div(baseline))
       pd_shock    <- clip(safe_div(shock))
       adjusted_pd <- stats::pnorm(
         stats::qnorm(pd_internal) +
         stats::qnorm(pd_shock) -
         stats::qnorm(pd_baseline)
       )
       ead * adjusted_pd
     }
   )
 }
 
 #' Aggregate EL integration results to portfolio level
 #'
 #' @param portfolio_df The `$portfolio` element from [integrate_el()].
 #' @param group_cols Character vector or NULL. NULL = portfolio total.
-#' @return A one-row tibble (per group) with total ELs + `el_adjusted_bps`.
+#' @return A one-row tibble (per group) with total ELs and two bps measures, both
+#'   as a loss rate over *notional exposure* (EL/EAD would be PD-in-bps, not a
+#'   loss rate): `el_adjusted_bps` — the adjusted EL *level* (total expected-loss
+#'   rate of the shocked book), and `el_adjustment_bps` — the climate overlay
+#'   (delta = adjusted - internal), the marginal transition effect.
 #' @export
 aggregate_el_integration <- function(portfolio_df, group_cols = NULL) {
   required <- c("internal_el", "expected_loss_baseline", "expected_loss_shock",
                 "trisk_adjusted_el", "exposure_value_usd")
   missing_cols <- setdiff(required, colnames(portfolio_df))
   if (length(missing_cols) > 0) {
     stop("aggregate_el_integration(): missing required columns: ",
          paste(missing_cols, collapse = ", "))
   }
 
   grouped <- if (is.null(group_cols)) {
     portfolio_df |> dplyr::mutate(.dummy = 1L) |> dplyr::group_by(.data$.dummy)
   } else {
     portfolio_df |> dplyr::group_by(dplyr::across(dplyr::all_of(group_cols)))
   }
 
   agg <- grouped |>
     dplyr::summarise(
       total_exposure_usd = sum(.data$exposure_value_usd, na.rm = TRUE),
       total_el_internal  = sum(.data$internal_el, na.rm = TRUE),
       total_el_baseline  = sum(.data$expected_loss_baseline, na.rm = TRUE),
       total_el_shock     = sum(.data$expected_loss_shock, na.rm = TRUE),
       total_el_adjusted  = sum(.data$trisk_adjusted_el, na.rm = TRUE),
       .groups = "drop"
     ) |>
     dplyr::mutate(
       total_el_adjustment = .data$total_el_adjusted - .data$total_el_internal,
+      # Both bps measures use *notional exposure* as the denominator: EL / exposure
+      # = LGD*PD in bps, a true loss rate. Dividing by EAD (= exposure * LGD) would
+      # instead yield PD-in-bps, not a loss rate (K1).
+      # el_adjusted_bps: the adjusted EL *level* as a loss rate (total expected loss
+      # of the shocked book = baseline credit risk + climate overlay).
       el_adjusted_bps     = el_to_bps(.data$total_el_adjusted,
+                                      .data$total_exposure_usd),
+      # el_adjustment_bps: the climate overlay (delta = adjusted - internal) as a
+      # loss rate — the marginal effect attributable to the transition scenario.
+      # Signed (el_to_bps returns a magnitude): positive = more loss, negative =
+      # less loss, so the direction of the delta is preserved.
+      el_adjustment_bps   = sign(.data$total_el_adjustment) *
+                            el_to_bps(.data$total_el_adjustment,
                                       .data$total_exposure_usd)
     )
 
   if (is.null(group_cols)) {
     agg <- agg |> dplyr::select(-dplyr::any_of(".dummy"))
   }
 
   tibble::as_tibble(agg)
 }

 #' @return A data frame containing the processed and analyzed portfolio data.

 run_trisk_on_portfolio <- function(assets_data,
                                    scenarios_data,

                                    carbon_data,

     )

     dplyr::mutate(company_id = as.character(.data$company_id))

+  warn_scenario_family_mismatch(baseline_scenario, target_scenario)  # NM1

     } else {

           assets_data = assets_data,

         )

         dplyr::filter(!is.na(.data$company_id)) |>

     }
   } else {
     portfolio_matched_companies <- portfolio_data |>
       dplyr::filter(!is.na(.data$company_id)) |>
       dplyr::distinct(.data$company_id, .data$country_iso2)
   }
 
   assets_data_filtered <- assets_data |>
     dplyr::inner_join(portfolio_matched_companies, by = c("company_id", "country_iso2"))
 
   cat("-- Start Trisk")
   st_results <- trisk.model::run_trisk_model(
     assets_data = assets_data_filtered,
     scenarios_data = scenarios_data,
     financial_data = financial_data,
     carbon_data = carbon_data,
     baseline_scenario = baseline_scenario,
     target_scenario = target_scenario,
     ...
   )
 
   npv_results <- st_results$npv_results |>
     dplyr::mutate(
       asset_id = as.character(.data$asset_id),
       company_id = as.character(.data$company_id)
     )

     dplyr::mutate(
       company_id = as.character(.data$company_id)
     )
 
+  # D1: warn (don't silently drop) when a portfolio term is outside the Merton grid.
+  warn_terms_outside_grid(portfolio_data, pd_results)
+
   analysis_data <- portfolio_data |>
     join_trisk_outputs_to_portfolio(npv_results = npv_results, pd_results = pd_results)

+  attr(analysis_data, "trisk_run_meta") <- build_trisk_run_meta(
+    baseline_scenario = baseline_scenario,

+    extra_args        = list(...)

 }
 
 #' Check Portfolio and Match Company IDs
 #'
 #' @description
 #' This function checks if the portfolio data contains all required columns and
 #' performs a fuzzy match to assign company IDs based on company names.
 #'
 #' @param portfolio_data Data frame containing portfolio information.
 #'
 #' @return A data frame of portfolio data with matched company IDs.
 #' @export
 check_portfolio <- function(portfolio_data) {
-  # List of required columns
-  required_portfolio_columns <- c("company_id", "company_name", "country_iso2", "exposure_value_usd", "term", "loss_given_default")
+  # Required columns for the FULL runner. sector + technology are mandatory here
+  # (V1): the runner joins TRISK outputs to the portfolio on them, so omitting
+  # them previously produced an opaque dplyr join error only after a full model
+  # run. They are deliberately NOT required by the simple runner
+  # (check_portfolio_simple), which allocates exposure across technologies by NPV
+  # share and needs no technology column on the input.
+  required_portfolio_columns <- c(
+    "company_id", "company_name", "country_iso2", "exposure_value_usd",
+    "term", "loss_given_default", "sector", "technology"
+  )
 
   # Check if all required columns are present
   if (!all(required_portfolio_columns %in% colnames(portfolio_data))) {
     missing_columns <- setdiff(required_portfolio_columns, colnames(portfolio_data))
     stop(paste("Error: Missing columns in portfolio_data:", paste(missing_columns, collapse = ", ")))
   }
 
   return(portfolio_data)
 }
 
 #' Fuzzy Match Company IDs
 #'
 #' @description
 #' This function performs a fuzzy match between portfolio company names and
 #' asset company names to assign company IDs to the portfolio data.
 #'
 #' @param portfolio_data Data frame containing portfolio information.
 #' @param assets_data Data frame containing asset information with company IDs.
-#' @param threshold Numeric value for the matching threshold. Default is 0.2.
-#' @param method tring specifying method to use for fuzzy matching. See help of stringdist::stringdistmatrix for possible values.
+#' @param threshold Numeric value for the matching threshold. Default is 0.5.
+#' @param method String specifying the method to use for fuzzy matching. See help of stringdist::stringdistmatrix for possible values.
 #'
 #' @return A data frame of portfolio data with fuzzy-matched company IDs.
 #' @export
 #'
 fuzzy_match_company_ids <- function(portfolio_data, assets_data, threshold = 0.5, method = "lcs") {
   companies_with_ids <- assets_data |>
     dplyr::distinct(.data$company_id, .data$company_name)
 
   # Perform normalized Levenshtein distance fuzzy matching
   matched_companies <- stringdist::stringdistmatrix(portfolio_data$company_name, companies_with_ids$company_name, method = method) |>
     as.data.frame() |>
     dplyr::mutate(portfolio_index = dplyr::row_number()) |>
     tidyr::pivot_longer(cols = -.data$portfolio_index, names_to = "npv_index", values_to = "distance") |>
     # Normalize the distance by dividing by the max string length between the portfolio and company name
     dplyr::mutate(
       normalized_distance = .data$distance /
         pmax(
           nchar(portfolio_data$company_name[.data$portfolio_index]),
           nchar(companies_with_ids$company_name[as.integer(gsub("V", "", .data$npv_index))])
         )
     ) |>
     # Group by the portfolio index and find the minimum normalized distance
     dplyr::group_by(.data$portfolio_index) |>
     dplyr::slice_min(order_by = .data$normalized_distance, n = 1) |>
     dplyr::ungroup() |>
     # Filter by the normalized threshold
     dplyr::filter(.data$normalized_distance <= threshold)
 
+  # CX2: slice_min() keeps ties, so a portfolio name equidistant from several
+  # company names would match all of them and duplicate that loan (full exposure
+  # applied to each). Warn naming the affected portfolio names and keep one match
+  # per portfolio row so exposure is not silently inflated.
+  tie_counts <- matched_companies |>
+    dplyr::count(.data$portfolio_index, name = "n_match") |>
+    dplyr::filter(.data$n_match > 1)
+  if (nrow(tie_counts) > 0) {
+    tied_names <- unique(portfolio_data$company_name[tie_counts$portfolio_index])
+    warning(
+      "fuzzy_match_company_ids(): ", nrow(tie_counts),
+      " portfolio name(s) tied across multiple companies at the same distance; ",
+      "keeping the first match each. Disambiguate by supplying company_id. ",
+      "Affected: ", paste(tied_names, collapse = ", "),
+      call. = FALSE
+    )
+    matched_companies <- matched_companies |>
+      dplyr::group_by(.data$portfolio_index) |>
+      dplyr::slice(1) |>
+      dplyr::ungroup()
+  }
+
   # Join the matched company_ids to the portfolio data
   portfolio_data_with_ids <- portfolio_data |>
     dplyr::mutate(portfolio_index = dplyr::row_number()) |>
     dplyr::left_join(matched_companies, by = "portfolio_index") |>
     dplyr::left_join(companies_with_ids |> dplyr::mutate(npv_index = paste0("V", dplyr::row_number())), by = "npv_index") |>
     dplyr::select(-"portfolio_index", -"npv_index", -"distance", -"company_name.y") |>
     dplyr::rename(company_name = .data$company_name.x)
 
   return(portfolio_data_with_ids)
 }
 
 #' Join TRISK Outputs to Portfolio
 #'
 #' @description
 #' This function joins the TRISK model outputs (NPV and PD results) to the portfolio data.
 #'
 #' @param portfolio_data Data frame containing portfolio information.
 #' @param npv_results Data frame containing NPV (Net Present Value) results from TRISK model.
 #' @param pd_results Data frame containing PD (Probability of Default) results from TRISK model.
 #'
 #' @return A data frame of portfolio data joined with TRISK model outputs.
 #' @export
 #'
 join_trisk_outputs_to_portfolio <- function(portfolio_data, npv_results, pd_results) {
+  # X1 fix: TRISK NPV output is asset-level, but the portfolio is joined without
+  # asset_id. Without this collapse, a company with multiple assets in one
+  # (sector, technology) fans a single loan into N rows and the full
+  # exposure_value_usd is then applied to each -> N x EAD/EL. Sum NPV across a
+  # company's assets within each (run, company, sector, technology, country) so
+  # every loan matches one row per technology and contributes its exposure once.
+  # Mirrors aggregate_trisk_outputs_simple() in the simple runner.
+  npv_results <- aggregate_npv_across_assets(npv_results)
+
   analysis_data <- dplyr::inner_join(
-    npv_results |> dplyr::select(-"company_name"),
+    npv_results,
     pd_results |> dplyr::select(-"company_name"),
     by = c("run_id", "company_id", "sector"),
     relationship = "many-to-many"
   )
 
 
   # Check if both company_name and country_name are NA
   if (any(is.na(portfolio_data$company_name)) & any(is.na(portfolio_data$company_id))) {
     # Aggregate facts for country only
     analysis_data <- analysis_data |>
       aggregate_facts_trisk(group_cols = c("country_iso2", "sector", "technology", "term"))
 
     # Define the join keys
     join_keys <- c("country_iso2", "sector", "technology", "term")
 
     # Merge the portfolio data
     full_joined_data <- merge_portfolio(portfolio_data, analysis_data, join_keys)
   } else {
     # Define the join keys including run_id and company_id
     join_keys <- c("company_id", "country_iso2", "sector", "technology", "term")
 
     # Merge the portfolio data
     full_joined_data <- merge_portfolio(portfolio_data, analysis_data, join_keys)
   }
 
 
   return(full_joined_data)
 }
 
 
+# Internal — collapse asset-level NPV to (run, company, sector, technology,
+# country) grain so a single portfolio loan does not fan out across a company's
+# assets (X1). NPV is summed across assets = the company-technology total. Other
+# columns (asset_id, asset_name, model-derived difference/change) are dropped;
+# net_present_value_difference and value-change metrics are recomputed downstream
+# by compute_analysis_metrics().
+aggregate_npv_across_assets <- function(npv_results) {
+  npv_results |>
+    dplyr::group_by(
+      .data$run_id, .data$company_id, .data$sector,
+      .data$technology, .data$country_iso2
+    ) |>
+    dplyr::summarise(
+      # Preserve NA for an all-NA group instead of collapsing to 0 (which would
+      # later divide into NaN/Inf in compute_analysis_metrics). Mirrors the
+      # all-NA guards in the simple runner's aggregation.
+      net_present_value_baseline = if (all(is.na(.data$net_present_value_baseline))) {
+        NA_real_
+      } else {
+        sum(.data$net_present_value_baseline, na.rm = TRUE)
+      },
+      net_present_value_shock = if (all(is.na(.data$net_present_value_shock))) {
+        NA_real_
+      } else {
+        sum(.data$net_present_value_shock, na.rm = TRUE)
+      },
+      .groups = "drop"
+    )
+}
+
 # Helper function to merge portfolio data based on the presence of term
 merge_portfolio <- function(portfolio, analysis, join_keys) {
   portfolio_with_term <- portfolio |> dplyr::filter(!is.na(.data$term))
   portfolio_without_term <- portfolio |> dplyr::filter(is.na(.data$term))
 
   # Merge portfolio_with_term including the term column
   merged_with_term <- portfolio_with_term |>
     dplyr::left_join(analysis, by = join_keys)
 
   # Filter analysis where term is 1 and drop the term column for the merge
   analysis_filtered <- analysis |>
     dplyr::filter(.data$term == 1) |>
     dplyr::select(-"term") |>
     dplyr::mutate(
       pd_baseline = NA_real_,
       pd_shock = NA_real_
     )
 
   # Merge portfolio_without_term without the term column
   merged_without_term <- portfolio_without_term |>
     dplyr::left_join(analysis_filtered, by = setdiff(join_keys, "term"))
 
   # Combine both merged datasets
   dplyr::bind_rows(merged_with_term, merged_without_term)
 }

    24	})

    31	test_that("integrate_el zscore returns positive magnitudes (post-59571f3 convention)", {
    32	  df <- make_test_analysis_data()
    33	  # Default internal_el = expected_loss_baseline (positive after 59571f3).
    34	  result <- integrate_el(df, method = "zscore")
    35	  expect_type(result, "list")
    36	  expect_equal(nrow(result$portfolio), nrow(df))
    37	  expect_true(all(is.finite(result$portfolio$trisk_adjusted_el)))
    38	  # Positive-magnitude convention: trisk_adjusted_el >= 0 for all rows.
    39	  expect_true(all(result$portfolio$trisk_adjusted_el >= 0),
    40	              info = "EL must be stored as positive magnitudes (matches expected_loss_*).")
    41	  # Numeric fingerprint: when internal == expected_loss_baseline, the z-score
    42	  # recombination collapses qnorm(pd_internal) - qnorm(pd_baseline_eff) to 0,
    43	  # so the recovered adjusted EL equals ead * pd_shock_eff = expected_loss_shock.
    44	  expect_equal(result$portfolio$trisk_adjusted_el,
    45	               c(2.0, 4.8, 1.8), tolerance = 1e-6)
    46	})

    52	  internal <- c(0.5, 2.0, 1.0)

   100	test_that("integrate_el zscore prefers exposure_at_default column over recomputing", {
   101	  # When a caller (e.g. run_trisk_on_simple_portfolio) supplies an
   102	  # exposure_at_default column derived from a scaled exposure
   103	  # (share * LGD instead of full * LGD), the zscore method must use that
   104	  # column as the canonical EAD denominator and multiplier.
   105	  #
   106	  # We exercise the non-degenerate path (internal != baseline) so the
   107	  # nonlinear qnorm transformation actually depends on the chosen
   108	  # denominator — otherwise the scaling cancels and the bug hides.
   109	
   110	  df <- make_test_analysis_data()
   111	  natural_ead <- df$exposure_value_usd * df$loss_given_default
   112	  df$exposure_at_default     <- 0.5 * natural_ead
   113	  df$expected_loss_baseline  <- df$exposure_at_default * df$pd_baseline
   114	  df$expected_loss_shock     <- df$exposure_at_default * df$pd_shock
   115	  internal_user <- 0.5 * df$expected_loss_baseline  # ≠ baseline → forces qnorm
   116	
   117	  result <- integrate_el(df, internal_el = internal_user, method = "zscore")
   118	
   119	  # Recompute the expected output using exposure_at_default as canonical EAD.
   120	  ead <- df$exposure_at_default
   121	  clip     <- function(x) pmin(pmax(x, 1e-4), 1 - 1e-4)
   122	  safe_div <- function(x) ifelse(ead > 0, abs(x) / ead, 0)
   123	  pd_int <- clip(safe_div(internal_user))
   124	  pd_bas <- clip(safe_div(df$expected_loss_baseline))
   125	  pd_sho <- clip(safe_div(df$expected_loss_shock))
   126	  adjusted_pd <- stats::pnorm(stats::qnorm(pd_int) +
   127	                              stats::qnorm(pd_sho) -
   128	                              stats::qnorm(pd_bas))
   129	  expected_el <- ead * adjusted_pd
   130	
   131	  expect_equal(result$portfolio$trisk_adjusted_el, expected_el, tolerance = 1e-6)
   132	})
